<h3>README / docs</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">export function getAuthTypeFromEnv(): AuthType | undefined {
  if (process.env['GOOGLE_GENAI_USE_GCA'] === 'true')
    return AuthType.LOGIN_WITH_GOOGLE;
  if (process.env['GOOGLE_GENAI_USE_VERTEXAI'] === 'true')
    return AuthType.USE_VERTEX_AI;
  if (process.env['GEMINI_API_KEY'])
    return AuthType.USE_GEMINI;
  if (process.env['CLOUD_SHELL'] === 'true' ||
      process.env['GEMINI_CLI_USE_COMPUTE_ADC'] === 'true')
    return AuthType.COMPUTE_ADC;
  return undefined;
}
</code></pre>

<pre><code class="language-typescript">export class CoreEventEmitter extends EventEmitter&#x3C;CoreEvents> {
  private _eventBacklog: EventBacklogItem[] = [];
  private _backlogHead = 0;
  private static readonly MAX_BACKLOG_SIZE = 10000;

  private _emitOrQueue&#x3C;K extends keyof CoreEvents>(event: K, ...args: CoreEvents[K]): void {
    if (this.listenerCount(event) === 0) {
      // 리스너 없으면 백로그에 큐잉 (최대 10,000개)
      // head 포인터로 O(1) 제거 + 주기적 컴팩션
    } else {
      this.emit(event, ...args);
    }
  }

  drainBacklogs(): void {
    // UI 구독 시 백로그된 이벤트 일괄 전달
  }
}
</code></pre>

<h2>코퍼스 — 013_etc/13_ge_etc.md (심화)</h2>
<h1>Gemini CLI 잔여 교차 관심사 분석</h1>
<h2>개요</h2>
<p>Gemini CLI는 Google이 개발한 터미널 기반 AI 코딩 에이전트로, 모노레포 구조(<code>packages/*</code>)에 7개 패키지를 포함한다. 본 문서는 차원 01-12(TUI, Prompt, Tool, Skill, Subagent, Surface, Sandbox, Config, MCP, Memory, Plugin, Guardian)에서 <strong>다루지 않은</strong> 잔여 교차 관심사 12개를 분석한다.</p>
<p><strong>패키지 구조:</strong></p>
<table>

<h2>1. Git/VCS 통합</h2>
<h3>1.1 GitService — Shadow Repository 체크포인팅</h3>
<p>Gemini CLI는 <code>simple-git</code> 라이브러리를 사용하여 <strong>섀도우 Git 저장소</strong> 기반 체크포인팅을 구현한다.</p>
<p><strong>핵심 파일:</strong> <code>/packages/core/src/services/gitService.ts</code></p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">export class GitService {
  private projectRoot: string;
  private storage: Storage;

  async setupShadowGitRepository() {
    const repoDir = this.getHistoryDir();
    const gitConfigContent =
      '[user]\n  name = Gemini CLI\n  email = gemini-cli@google.com\n[commit]\n  gpgsign = false\n';
    await fs.writeFile(gitConfigPath, gitConfigContent);

    const repo = simpleGit(repoDir).env(shadowRepoEnv);
    if (!isRepoDefined) {
      await repo.init(false, { '--initial-branch': 'main' });
      await repo.commit('Initial commit', { '--allow-empty': null });
    }
  }

  private get shadowGitRepository(): SimpleGit {
    return simpleGit(this.projectRoot).env({
      GIT_DIR: path.join(repoDir, '.git'),
      GIT_WORK_TREE: this.projectRoot,
      ...this.getShadowRepoEnv(repoDir),
    });
  }

  async createFileSnapshot(message: string): Promise&#x3C;string> {
    const repo = this.shadowGitRepository;
    await repo.add('.');
    const status = await repo.status();
    if (status.isClean()) return await this.getCurrentCommitHash();
    const commitResult = await repo.commit(message, { '--no-verify': null });
    return commitResult.commit;
  }

  async restoreProjectFromSnapshot(commitHash: string): Promise&#x3C;void> {
    const repo = this.shadowGitRepository;
    await repo.raw(['restore', '--source', commitHash, '.']);
    await repo.clean('f', ['-d']);
  }
}
</code></pre>
<p><strong>설계 특징:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>사용자의 <code>.git</code> 저장소와 <strong>완전 분리</strong>된 섀도우 저장소 운영</li>
<li><code>GIT_CONFIG_GLOBAL</code>/<code>GIT_CONFIG_SYSTEM</code> 환경변수로 사용자 git 설정 격리</li>
<li><code>gpgsign = false</code>로 GPG 서명 비활성화</li>
<li>프로젝트 <code>.gitignore</code> 파일을 섀도우 저장소에 복사하여 동일한 무시 패턴 적용</li>
</ul>
<h3>1.2 .gitignore 파싱</h3>
<p><strong>핵심 파일:</strong> <code>/packages/core/src/utils/gitIgnoreParser.ts</code>, <code>/packages/core/src/utils/ignorePatterns.ts</code></p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">export const COMMON_IGNORE_PATTERNS: string[] = [
  '**/node_modules/**',
  '**/.git/**',
  '**/bower_components/**',
  '**/.svn/**',
  '**/.hg/**',
];
</code></pre>
<p>파일 검색 도구 전반에서 <code>.gitignore</code> 패턴을 존중하며, <code>file_filtering_respect_git_ignore</code> 설정으로 제어 가능하다.</p>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">flowchart TD
    A[GitService] --> B[Shadow Git Repo]
    B --> C[createFileSnapshot]
    B --> D[restoreProjectFromSnapshot]
    C --> E[git add . + git commit]
    D --> F[git restore --source + git clean]
    G[ignorePatterns] --> H[COMMON_IGNORE_PATTERNS]
    G --> I[gitIgnoreParser]
    I --> J[파일 검색 도구들]
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>2. 모델 라우팅 / 프로바이더 추상화</h2>
<h3>2.1 ModelRouterService — 복합 전략 패턴</h3>
<p>Gemini CLI의 모델 라우팅은 <strong>Strategy 패턴 + Chain of Responsibility</strong> 조합으로 구현되어 있다. 이는 다른 CLI 에이전트에서 찾아보기 어려운 정교한 구조이다.</p>
<p><strong>핵심 파일:</strong> <code>/packages/core/src/routing/modelRouterService.ts</code></p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">export class ModelRouterService {
  private strategy: TerminalStrategy;

  private initializeDefaultStrategy(): TerminalStrategy {
    const strategies: RoutingStrategy[] = [];
    strategies.push(new FallbackStrategy());     // 1. 가용성 기반 폴백
    strategies.push(new OverrideStrategy());     // 2. 사용자 오버라이드
    strategies.push(new ApprovalModeStrategy()); // 3. 승인 모드 라우팅
    if (this.config.getGemmaModelRouterSettings()?.enabled) {
      strategies.push(new GemmaClassifierStrategy()); // 4. Gemma 로컬 분류기
    }
    strategies.push(new ClassifierStrategy());         // 5. LLM 기반 분류기
    strategies.push(new NumericalClassifierStrategy()); // 6. 수치 분류기
    const terminalStrategy = new DefaultStrategy();     // 7. 기본 전략(종단)
    return new CompositeStrategy([...strategies, terminalStrategy], 'agent-router');
  }
}
</code></pre>
<h3>2.2 라우팅 전략 계층</h3>
<p><strong>핵심 파일:</strong> <code>/packages/core/src/routing/routingStrategy.ts</code></p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">export interface RoutingDecision {
  model: string;
  metadata: {
    source: string;
    latencyMs: number;
    reasoning: string;
    error?: string;
  };
}

export interface RoutingStrategy {
  readonly name: string;
  route(context: RoutingContext, config: Config,
        baseLlmClient: BaseLlmClient,
        localLiteRtLmClient: LocalLiteRtLmClient
  ): Promise&#x3C;RoutingDecision | null>;
}

export interface TerminalStrategy extends RoutingStrategy {
  route(...): Promise&#x3C;RoutingDecision>; // null 반환 불가
}
</code></pre>
<h3>2.3 ClassifierStrategy — Flash vs Pro 라우팅</h3>
<p><strong>핵심 파일:</strong> <code>/packages/core/src/routing/strategies/classifierStrategy.ts</code></p>
<p>LLM을 사용해 작업 복잡도를 판별하고, Flash(단순) 또는 Pro(복잡)으로 라우팅한다:</p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">const CLASSIFIER_SYSTEM_PROMPT = `
You are a specialized Task Routing AI. Choose between \`flash\` (SIMPLE) or \`pro\` (COMPLEX).
A task is COMPLEX if it meets ONE OR MORE:
1. High Operational Complexity (Est. 4+ Steps/Tool Calls)
2. Strategic Planning &#x26; Conceptual Design
3. High Ambiguity or Large Scope
4. Deep Debugging &#x26; Root Cause Analysis
`;
</code></pre>
<h3>2.4 가용성 기반 폴백</h3>
<p><strong>핵심 파일:</strong> <code>/packages/core/src/availability/modelPolicy.ts</code>, <code>/packages/core/src/fallback/handler.ts</code></p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">export type FailureKind = 'terminal' | 'transient' | 'not_found' | 'unknown';
export type FallbackAction = 'silent' | 'prompt';

export interface ModelPolicy {
  model: ModelId;
  actions: ModelPolicyActionMap;
  stateTransitions: ModelPolicyStateMap;

}
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">flowchart TD
    A[route 요청] --> B{FallbackStrategy}
    B -->|모델 가용| C{OverrideStrategy}
    B -->|모델 불가| Z[대체 모델 선택]
    C -->|오버라이드 없음| D{ApprovalModeStrategy}
    C -->|오버라이드 있음| Z2[오버라이드 모델]
    D --> E{GemmaClassifierStrategy}
    E --> F{ClassifierStrategy}
    F --> G{NumericalClassifierStrategy}
    G --> H[DefaultStrategy - 종단]

    style B fill:#f96
    style H fill:#6f9
</code></pre>

<h2>3. 에러 처리 / 복구 패턴</h2>
<h3>3.1 에러 타입 계층</h3>

<pre><code class="language-typescript">// Fatal 에러 계층 (프로세스 종료 유도)
FatalError (exitCode)
  ├── FatalAuthenticationError (41)
  ├── FatalInputError (42)
  ├── FatalSandboxError (44)
  ├── FatalConfigError (52)
  ├── FatalTurnLimitedError (53)
  ├── FatalToolExecutionError (54)
  └── FatalCancellationError (130 = SIGINT)

// 비-fatal 에러

  └── AccountSuspendedError (appealUrl 포함)

<h3>3.2 Quota 에러 분류</h3>
<p><strong>핵심 파일:</strong> <code>/packages/core/src/utils/googleQuotaErrors.ts</code></p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">export class TerminalQuotaError extends Error {
  retryDelayMs?: number;
  reason?: string;
  get isInsufficientCredits(): boolean {
    return this.reason === 'INSUFFICIENT_G1_CREDITS_BALANCE';
  }
}

export class RetryableQuotaError extends Error {
  retryDelayMs?: number;
}

export class ValidationRequiredError extends Error {
  validationLink?: string;
  validationDescription?: string;
  userHandled: boolean = false;
}
</code></pre>
<h3>3.3 재시도 엔진 — retryWithBackoff</h3>
<p><strong>핵심 파일:</strong> <code>/packages/core/src/utils/retry.ts</code></p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">export const DEFAULT_MAX_ATTEMPTS = 10;

export interface RetryOptions {
  maxAttempts: number;        // 기본값 10
  initialDelayMs: number;     // 기본값 5000ms
  maxDelayMs: number;         // 기본값 30000ms (30초)
  shouldRetryOnError: (error: Error) => boolean;
  shouldRetryOnContent?: (content: GenerateContentResponse) => boolean;
  onPersistent429?: (authType?, error?) => Promise&#x3C;string | boolean | null>;
  onValidationRequired?: (error) => Promise&#x3C;'verify' | 'change_auth' | 'cancel'>;
  signal?: AbortSignal;
  getAvailabilityContext?: () => RetryAvailabilityContext | undefined;
}
</code></pre>
<p><strong>재시도 가능 네트워크 에러 코드:</strong></p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">const RETRYABLE_NETWORK_CODES = [
  'ECONNRESET', 'ETIMEDOUT', 'EPIPE', 'ENOTFOUND', 'EAI_AGAIN',
  'ECONNREFUSED', 'ERR_SSL_SSLV3_ALERT_BAD_RECORD_MAC',
  'ERR_SSL_WRONG_VERSION_NUMBER', 'ERR_SSL_DECRYPTION_FAILED_OR_BAD_RECORD_MAC',
  'ERR_SSL_BAD_RECORD_MAC', 'EPROTO',
];
</code></pre>
<p><strong>재시도 흐름:</strong></p>
<ol>
<li><code>TerminalQuotaError</code> / <code>ModelNotFoundError</code> -> <code>onPersistent429</code> 콜백으로 모델 폴백 시도</li>
<li><code>ValidationRequiredError</code> -> <code>onValidationRequired</code> 콜백으로 사용자 검증 유도</li>
<li><code>RetryableQuotaError</code> / 5xx -> 서버 지정 <code>retryDelayMs</code> 존중 + 지수 백오프</li>
<li>기타 재시도 가능 에러 -> 지수 백오프 + jitter(+-30%)</li>
</ol>
<h3>3.4 Fallback Handler</h3>
<p><strong>핵심 파일:</strong> <code>/packages/core/src/fallback/handler.ts</code></p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">export type FallbackIntent =
  | 'retry_always'     // 폴백 모델로 영구 전환
  | 'retry_once'       // 이번 턴만 폴백
  | 'retry_with_credits'
  | 'stop'
  | 'retry_later'
  | 'upgrade';         // 브라우저로 업그레이드 페이지 열기
</code></pre>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">flowchart TD
    E[API 에러 발생] --> F{classifyGoogleError}
    F -->|TerminalQuotaError| G[onPersistent429]
    F -->|ValidationRequired| H[onValidationRequired]
    F -->|RetryableQuota/5xx| I[지수 백오프 재시도]
    F -->|네트워크 에러| I
    G --> J{handleFallback}
    J --> K[resolvePolicyChain]
    K --> L{FallbackIntent}
    L -->|retry_always| M[activateFallbackMode]
    L -->|upgrade| N[openBrowserSecurely]
    L -->|stop| O[중단]
</code></pre>

<h2>4. 텔레메트리 / 관측성</h2>
<h3>4.1 OpenTelemetry 기반 계측</h3>
<p>Gemini CLI는 <strong>OpenTelemetry SDK</strong> 전체 스택(트레이스, 메트릭, 로그)을 채택한 가장 완전한 텔레메트리 구현 중 하나이다.</p>
<p><strong>핵심 파일들:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li><code>/packages/core/src/telemetry/sdk.ts</code> — SDK 초기화</li>
<li><code>/packages/core/src/telemetry/metrics.ts</code> — 메트릭 정의</li>
<li><code>/packages/core/src/telemetry/loggers.ts</code> — 로그 이벤트</li>
<li><code>/packages/core/src/telemetry/trace.ts</code> — 분산 트레이싱</li>
<li><code>/packages/core/src/telemetry/semantic.ts</code> — OTel GenAI 시맨틱 컨벤션</li>
</ul>
<p><strong>텔레메트리 대상 (TelemetryTarget):</strong></p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">export enum TelemetryTarget {
  GCP = 'gcp',     // Google Cloud로 전송
  LOCAL = 'local',  // 로컬 OTLP 엔드포인트
}
</code></pre>
<h3>4.2 메트릭 카탈로그</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 핵심 메트릭
'gemini_cli.tool.call.count'
'gemini_cli.tool.call.latency'
'gemini_cli.api.request.count'
'gemini_cli.api.request.latency'
'gemini_cli.token.usage'
'gemini_cli.session.count'
'gemini_cli.file.operation.count'
'gemini_cli.lines.changed'
'gemini_cli.network_retry.count'
'gemini_cli.model_routing.latency'

// 에이전트 메트릭
'gemini_cli.agent.run.count'
'gemini_cli.agent.duration'
'gemini_cli.agent.turns'
'gemini_cli.agent.recovery_attempt.count'

// OTel GenAI 시맨틱 컨벤션
'gen_ai.client.token.usage'
'gen_ai.client.operation.duration'

// 성능 모니터링
'gemini_cli.startup.duration'
'gemini_cli.memory.usage'
'gemini_cli.cpu.usage'
'gemini_cli.performance.score'
'gemini_cli.performance.regression'
</code></pre>
<h3>4.3 분산 트레이싱</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">export async function runInDevTraceSpan&#x3C;R>(
  opts: SpanOptions &#x26; { operation: GeminiCliOperation; logPrompts?: boolean },
  fn: ({ metadata }: { metadata: SpanMetadata }) => Promise&#x3C;R>,
): Promise&#x3C;R> {
  const tracer = trace.getTracer('gemini-cli', 'v1');
  return tracer.startActiveSpan(operation, restOfSpanOpts, async (span) => {
    // 자동으로 input/output/error 기록
    // AsyncIterable(스트림) 응답도 래핑하여 스트림 완료 시 span 종료
  });
}
</code></pre>
<h3>4.4 Clearcut Logger</h3>
<p><strong>핵심 파일:</strong> <code>/packages/core/src/telemetry/clearcut-logger/clearcut-logger.ts</code></p>
<p>Google 내부 분석 시스템(Clearcut)으로 이벤트를 전송하는 전용 로거. 시스템 정보(OS, CPU)와 함께 60종 이상의 텔레메트리 이벤트를 수집한다.</p>
<h3>4.5 StartupProfiler</h3>
<p><strong>핵심 파일:</strong> <code>/packages/core/src/telemetry/startupProfiler.ts</code></p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">export class StartupProfiler {
  private phases: Map&#x3C;string, StartupPhase> = new Map();
  // 각 시작 단계(config 로드, auth, 도구 등록 등)의 소요 시간과 CPU 사용량 측정
}
</code></pre>
<h3>4.6 활동 모니터링</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// ActivityDetector — 사용자 활동 감지
// ActivityMonitor — 유휴 상태 추적
// MemoryMonitor — 메모리 사용량 모니터링
// HighWaterMarkTracker — 최대치 추적
// RateLimiter — 요청 속도 제한
</code></pre>

<h2>5. IDE 통합 (Gemini의 강점)</h2>
<h3>5.1 아키텍처</h3>
<p>Gemini CLI의 IDE 통합은 <strong>MCP 프로토콜 기반 클라이언트-서버</strong> 구조로, 업계에서 가장 정교한 IDE 연동 중 하나이다.</p>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">flowchart LR
    subgraph "VS Code Extension"
        A[extension.ts] --> B[IDEServer]
        B --> C[DiffManager]
        B --> D[OpenFilesManager]
        B --> E[McpServer via StreamableHTTP]
    end

    subgraph "Gemini CLI Core"
        F[IdeClient] --> G[ideContext Store]
        F --> H[MCP Client Transport]
    end

    H &#x3C;-->|MCP Protocol| E

    subgraph "지원 IDE"
        I[VS Code]
        J[Cursor]
        K[Firebase Studio]
        L[JetBrains IDEs]
        M[Zed]
        N[Sublime Text]
        O[Xcode]
    end
</code></pre>
<h3>5.2 IDE 자동 감지</h3>
<p><strong>핵심 파일:</strong> <code>/packages/core/src/ide/detect-ide.ts</code></p>
<p><strong>20개 이상의 IDE/환경</strong> 자동 감지:</p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">export const IDE_DEFINITIONS = {
  devin: { name: 'devin', displayName: 'Devin' },
  replit: { name: 'replit', displayName: 'Replit' },
  cursor: { name: 'cursor', displayName: 'Cursor' },
  cloudshell: { name: 'cloudshell', displayName: 'Cloud Shell' },
  codespaces: { name: 'codespaces', displayName: 'GitHub Codespaces' },
  firebasestudio: { name: 'firebasestudio', displayName: 'Firebase Studio' },
  vscode: { name: 'vscode', displayName: 'VS Code' },
  positron: { name: 'positron', displayName: 'Positron' },
  jetbrains: { name: 'jetbrains', displayName: 'JetBrains IDE' },
  intellijidea: { name: 'intellijidea', displayName: 'IntelliJ IDEA' },
  webstorm: { name: 'webstorm', displayName: 'WebStorm' },
  pycharm: { name: 'pycharm', displayName: 'PyCharm' },
  zed: { name: 'zed', displayName: 'Zed' },
  xcode: { name: 'xcode', displayName: 'XCode' },
  // ... 등
};
</code></pre>
<p>환경 변수 기반 감지 로직: <code>CURSOR_TRACE_ID</code>, <code>REPLIT_USER</code>, <code>MONOSPACE_ENV</code>, <code>ZED_SESSION_ID</code> 등.</p>
<h3>5.3 VS Code IDE Companion 확장</h3>

<ul>
<li><strong>MCP over StreamableHTTP</strong> 전송 계층 사용</li>
<li>Express 기반 HTTP 서버 + CORS 보안</li>
<li>인증 토큰(<code>GEMINI_CLI_IDE_AUTH_TOKEN</code>)으로 보안</li>
<li>포트 파일 기반 서비스 디스커버리</li>
</ul>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">const MCP_SESSION_ID_HEADER = 'mcp-session-id';
const IDE_SERVER_PORT_ENV_VAR = 'GEMINI_CLI_IDE_SERVER_PORT';
const IDE_WORKSPACE_PATH_ENV_VAR = 'GEMINI_CLI_IDE_WORKSPACE_PATH';

<h2>6. 패키징 / 배포</h2>
<h3>6.1 모노레포 구조</h3>
<p><strong>핵심 파일:</strong> <code>/package.json</code></p>
<pre><code class="language-json">{
  "name": "@google/gemini-cli",
  "version": "0.36.0-nightly.20260317.2f90b4653",
  "workspaces": ["packages/*"],
  "bin": { "gemini": "bundle/gemini.js" },
  "files": ["bundle/", "README.md", "LICENSE"]
}
</code></pre>
<h3>6.2 빌드 파이프라인</h3>
<pre><code>npm run generate → git commit info 생성
npm run bundle   → esbuild로 단일 번들 생성
npm run build    → 전체 패키지 빌드
npm run build:sandbox → Docker 샌드박스 이미지 빌드
npm run build:vscode  → VS Code 확장 빌드
npm run build:binary  → SEA(Single Executable Application) 바이너리 생성
</code></pre>
<h3>6.3 SEA (Single Executable Application)</h3>
<p><strong>핵심 파일:</strong> <code>/sea/sea-launch.cjs</code></p>
<p>Node.js SEA 기능을 활용한 단일 바이너리 배포 지원.</p>
<h3>6.4 esbuild 번들링</h3>
<p><strong>핵심 파일:</strong> <code>/esbuild.config.js</code></p>
<p>esbuild를 사용하여 모든 패키지를 <code>bundle/gemini.js</code> 단일 파일로 번들링. <code>ink</code> 라이브러리는 <code>@jrichman/ink</code> 포크 사용.</p>
<h3>6.5 Docker 샌드박스 이미지</h3>
<pre><code class="language-json">{
  "config": {
    "sandboxImageUri": "us-docker.pkg.dev/gemini-code-dev/130_gemini-cli/sandbox:0.36.0-..."
  }
}
</code></pre>

  if (env['CI']) return 60000;         // CI: 1분

<h2>8. 인증 / API 키 관리</h2>
<h3>8.1 인증 타입 6가지</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">export enum AuthType {
  LOGIN_WITH_GOOGLE = 'oauth-personal',      // Google OAuth
  USE_GEMINI = 'gemini-api-key',             // API 키
  USE_VERTEX_AI = 'vertex-ai',              // Vertex AI
  LEGACY_CLOUD_SHELL = 'cloud-shell',       // Cloud Shell (레거시)
  COMPUTE_ADC = 'compute-default-credentials', // 컴퓨트 기본 자격증명
  GATEWAY = 'gateway',                       // 게이트웨이
}
</code></pre>
<h3>8.2 환경 변수 기반 자동 감지</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">export function getAuthTypeFromEnv(): AuthType | undefined {
  if (process.env['GOOGLE_GENAI_USE_GCA'] === 'true')
    return AuthType.LOGIN_WITH_GOOGLE;
  if (process.env['GOOGLE_GENAI_USE_VERTEXAI'] === 'true')
    return AuthType.USE_VERTEX_AI;
  if (process.env['GEMINI_API_KEY'])
    return AuthType.USE_GEMINI;
  if (process.env['CLOUD_SHELL'] === 'true' ||
      process.env['GEMINI_CLI_USE_COMPUTE_ADC'] === 'true')
    return AuthType.COMPUTE_ADC;
  return undefined;
}
</code></pre>
<h3>8.3 OAuth 2.0 + PKCE</h3>
<p><strong>핵심 파일:</strong> <code>/packages/core/src/utils/oauth-flow.ts</code></p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">export interface OAuthFlowConfig {
  clientId: string;
  clientSecret?: string;
  authorizationUrl: string;
  tokenUrl: string;
  scopes?: string[];
  audiences?: string[];
  redirectUri?: string;
}

export function generatePKCEParams(): PKCEParams { ... }
</code></pre>
<p>완전한 OAuth 2.0 Authorization Code + PKCE 플로우 구현. 로컬 HTTP 콜백 서버(<code>/oauth/callback</code>) 운영.</p>
<h3>8.4 동의 관리</h3>
<p><strong>핵심 파일:</strong> <code>/packages/core/src/utils/authConsent.ts</code></p>
<p>대화형 모드(TUI)와 비대화형 모드(headless) 모두 지원하는 OAuth 동의 플로우.</p>
<h3>8.5 토큰 저장</h3>
<p><code>keytar</code> (OS 키체인), MCP 토큰 저장소 등 다중 토큰 저장 백엔드 지원. 키체인 가용성 텔레메트리도 수집한다.</p>

<h2>9. 음성 / 멀티모달</h2>
<h3>9.1 Voice Response Formatter</h3>
<p><strong>핵심 파일:</strong> <code>/packages/core/src/voice/responseFormatter.ts</code></p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">export interface FormatForSpeechOptions {
  maxLength?: number;     // 기본 500자
  pathDepth?: number;     // 기본 3 세그먼트
  jsonThreshold?: number; // 기본 80자
}
</code></pre>
<p>모델 응답을 음성 출력에 적합하게 변환:</p>
<ul>
<li>ANSI 이스케이프 시퀀스 제거</li>
<li>Markdown 문법(코드 펜스, 볼드, 헤딩 등) 제거</li>
<li>스택 트레이스 요약</li>
<li>절대 경로 축약</li>
<li>JSON 값 요약</li>
</ul>
<h3>9.2 이미지/미디어 파일 지원</h3>
<p><strong>핵심 파일:</strong> <code>/packages/core/src/utils/ignorePatterns.ts</code></p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">export const MEDIA_FILE_PATTERNS: string[] = [
  '**/*.pdf', '**/*.png', '**/*.jpg', '**/*.jpeg', // ...
];
</code></pre>
<p>미디어 파일은 <code>inlineData</code>로 변환하여 Gemini API에 전달. <code>read-file</code>, <code>read-many-files</code> 도구에서 이미지/PDF를 바이너리 데이터로 읽어 멀티모달 입력으로 제공한다.</p>
<hr>
<h2>10. 이벤트 시스템</h2>
<h3>10.1 CoreEventEmitter — 타입 안전 이벤트 버스</h3>
<p><strong>핵심 파일:</strong> <code>/packages/core/src/utils/events.ts</code></p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">export enum CoreEvent {
  UserFeedback = 'user-feedback',
  ModelChanged = 'model-changed',
  ConsoleLog = 'console-log',
  Output = 'output',
  MemoryChanged = 'memory-changed',
  ExternalEditorClosed = 'external-editor-closed',
  McpClientUpdate = 'mcp-client-update',
  OauthDisplayMessage = 'oauth-display-message',
  SettingsChanged = 'settings-changed',
  HookStart = 'hook-start',
  HookEnd = 'hook-end',
  AgentsRefreshed = 'agents-refreshed',
  AdminSettingsChanged = 'admin-settings-changed',
  RetryAttempt = 'retry-attempt',
  ConsentRequest = 'consent-request',
  McpProgress = 'mcp-progress',
  AgentsDiscovered = 'agents-discovered',
  RequestEditorSelection = 'request-editor-selection',
  EditorSelected = 'editor-selected',
  SlashCommandConflicts = 'slash-command-conflicts',
  QuotaChanged = 'quota-changed',
  TelemetryKeychainAvailability = 'telemetry-keychain-availability',
  TelemetryTokenStorageType = 'telemetry-token-storage-type',
}
</code></pre>
<h3>10.2 이벤트 백로그 시스템</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">export class CoreEventEmitter extends EventEmitter&#x3C;CoreEvents> {
  private _eventBacklog: EventBacklogItem[] = [];
  private _backlogHead = 0;
  private static readonly MAX_BACKLOG_SIZE = 10000;

  private _emitOrQueue&#x3C;K extends keyof CoreEvents>(event: K, ...args: CoreEvents[K]): void {
    if (this.listenerCount(event) === 0) {
      // 리스너 없으면 백로그에 큐잉 (최대 10,000개)
      // head 포인터로 O(1) 제거 + 주기적 컴팩션
    } else {
      this.emit(event, ...args);
    }
  }

  drainBacklogs(): void {
    // UI 구독 시 백로그된 이벤트 일괄 전달
  }
}
</code></pre>
<p><strong>특징:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>TypeScript 제네릭으로 <strong>타입 안전</strong> 이벤트 시그니처</li>
<li>UI 미구독 시 <strong>자동 백로깅</strong> (최대 10,000개)</li>
<li>Head 포인터 기반 <strong>O(1) 제거</strong> + 50% 임계치 컴팩션</li>
<li>싱글턴 <code>coreEvents</code> 인스턴스</li>
</ul>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">flowchart TD
    A[Core 모듈] -->|emitFeedback| B[CoreEventEmitter]
    A -->|emitRetryAttempt| B
    A -->|emitModelChanged| B
    B -->|리스너 있음| C[즉시 emit]
    B -->|리스너 없음| D[백로그 큐]
    D -->|drainBacklogs| E[UI 구독 후 일괄 전달]
    C --> F[TUI Renderer]
    E --> F
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>11. 피처 플래그 / 실험</h2>
<h3>11.1 실험 시스템</h3>
<p><strong>핵심 파일:</strong> <code>/packages/core/src/code_assist/experiments/experiments.ts</code></p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">export interface Experiments {
  flags: Record&#x3C;string, Flag>;
  experimentIds: number[];
}

export async function getExperiments(server?: CodeAssistServer): Promise&#x3C;Experiments> {
  // 1. GEMINI_EXP 환경변수로 로컬 파일에서 로드
  // 2. CodeAssist 서버에서 원격 페치
  // 캐싱되어 세션당 1회만 호출
}
</code></pre>
<h3>11.2 플래그 카탈로그</h3>
<p><strong>핵심 파일:</strong> <code>/packages/core/src/code_assist/experiments/flagNames.ts</code></p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">export const ExperimentFlags = {
  CONTEXT_COMPRESSION_THRESHOLD: 45740197,
  USER_CACHING: 45740198,
  BANNER_TEXT_NO_CAPACITY_ISSUES: 45740199,
  BANNER_TEXT_CAPACITY_ISSUES: 45740200,
  ENABLE_PREVIEW: 45740196,
  ENABLE_NUMERICAL_ROUTING: 45750526,
  CLASSIFIER_THRESHOLD: 45750527,
  ENABLE_ADMIN_CONTROLS: 45752213,
  MASKING_PROTECTION_THRESHOLD: 45758817,
  MASKING_PRUNABLE_THRESHOLD: 45758818,
  MASKING_PROTECT_LATEST_TURN: 45758819,
  GEMINI_3_1_PRO_LAUNCHED: 45760185,
  PRO_MODEL_NO_ACCESS: 45768879,
} as const;
</code></pre>
<p><strong>특징:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>숫자 ID 기반 플래그 (Google 내부 실험 시스템 연동)</li>
<li><code>GEMINI_EXP</code> 환경변수로 로컬 오버라이드 가능</li>
<li>라우팅 전략, 컨텍스트 압축, 마스킹 임계값 등 핵심 동작 제어</li>
<li>CodeAssist 서버에서 원격으로 실험 할당</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h2>12. 국제화 / 접근성</h2>
<h3>12.1 현재 상태</h3>
<p>Gemini CLI는 <strong>명시적 i18n 프레임워크가 없다</strong>. 모든 사용자 대면 문자열은 영어 하드코딩이다. 별도의 메시지 카탈로그나 번역 파일은 존재하지 않는다.</p>
<h3>12.2 접근성 관련 요소</h3>
<ul>
<li><strong>시스템 인코딩 감지:</strong> <code>/packages/core/src/utils/systemEncoding.ts</code> — 터미널 인코딩 자동 감지</li>
<li><strong>Voice Response Formatter:</strong> 음성 출력을 위한 텍스트 정제 (접근성 간접 지원)</li>
<li><strong>Headless 모드:</strong> <code>/packages/core/src/utils/headless.ts</code> — 비대화형 환경 지원</li>
<li><strong>테마:</strong> Ink 기반 TUI에서 터미널 색상 스킴 따름</li>
</ul>
<h3>12.3 부재 요소</h3>
<ul>
<li>다국어 메시지 카탈로그 없음</li>
<li>RTL(오른쪽에서 왼쪽) 텍스트 지원 없음</li>
<li>스크린 리더 호환 ARIA 레이블 없음 (TUI 특성상 제한적)</li>
<li>로케일 기반 날짜/숫자 포매팅 없음</li>
</ul>
<hr>

<h3>타 에이전트 대비 차별점</h3>
<ol>
<li><strong>모델 라우팅</strong>: 작업 복잡도에 따른 자동 모델 선택은 Gemini CLI만의 독자적 기능. Claude Code/OpenAI Codex에는 동등한 라우팅 계층이 없다.</li>
<li><strong>IDE 통합 깊이</strong>: MCP 프로토콜 기반으로 VS Code 내 diff 뷰, 파일 추적까지 지원하는 수준은 Claude Code의 VS Code 확장보다 더 깊은 통합이다.</li>
<li><strong>텔레메트리 성숙도</strong>: OTel 전체 스택 + Google Clearcut 이중 파이프라인은 분석 인프라 측면에서 가장 완전한 구현이다.</li>
<li><strong>가용성/폴백 정책</strong>: 모델별 상태 머신(healthy/transient/terminal) + 정책 체인 기반 자동 폴백은 프로덕션급 복원력을 제공한다.</li>
</ol>

4c:T530e,<h2>기초 설명</h2>
<p>Gemini CLI exposes web research as two complementary builtins: <strong><code>google_web_search</code></strong> (grounded search synthesis) and <strong><code>web_fetch</code></strong> (multi-URL deep read). Search execution is <strong>API-hosted</strong> — the CLI calls <code>geminiClient.generateContent</code> with model id <code>'web-search'</code> and parses <code>groundingMetadata</code> from the response.</p>

<h2>코퍼스 — 014_web-search/14_ge_web-search.md (심화)</h2>
<h1>Gemini CLI — Web Search 구현</h1>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>분석 스냅샷</strong>: <code>130_gemini-cli/</code> — <code>google_web_search</code> declarative tool + Google Search Grounding via Gemini API utility model.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Gemini CLI exposes web research as two complementary builtins: <strong><code>google_web_search</code></strong> (grounded search synthesis) and <strong><code>web_fetch</code></strong> (multi-URL deep read). Search execution is <strong>API-hosted</strong> — the CLI calls <code>geminiClient.generateContent</code> with model id <code>'web-search'</code> and parses <code>groundingMetadata</code> from the response.</p>
<h2>Architecture</h2>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">flowchart LR
  Agent["Agent loop"] --> WST["WebSearchTool.execute"]
  WST --> API["geminiClient.generateContent model: web-search"]
  API --> Ground["groundingMetadata"]
  Ground --> Chunks["groundingChunks uri/title"]
  Ground --> Supports["groundingSupports → citation markers"]
  WST --> Result["llmContent + Sources list"]
  Agent --> WF["web_fetch — separate tool"]
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>1. Tool identity &#x26; declaration</h2>
<h3>Name constants</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 130_gemini-cli/packages/core/src/tools/definitions/base-declarations.ts:71-73
export const WEB_SEARCH_TOOL_NAME = 'google_web_search';
export const WEB_SEARCH_PARAM_QUERY = 'query';
</code></pre>
<h3>Gemini 3 model-family schema</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 130_gemini-cli/packages/core/src/tools/definitions/model-family-sets/gemini-3.ts:396-410
google_web_search: {
  name: WEB_SEARCH_TOOL_NAME,
  description: `Performs a grounded Google Search...`,
  parametersJsonSchema: {
    type: 'object',
    properties: { query: { type: 'string', /* ... */ } },
    required: [WEB_SEARCH_PARAM_QUERY],
  },
},
</code></pre>
<p>Legacy models use parallel definition in <code>default-legacy.ts:413+</code>. Resolver: <code>coreTools.ts:157-159</code> (<code>resolveToolDeclaration</code> per model id).</p>
<h3>Tool class</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 130_gemini-cli/packages/core/src/tools/web-search.ts:206-210
export class WebSearchTool extends BaseDeclarativeTool&#x3C;WebSearchToolParams, WebSearchToolResult> {
  static readonly Name = WEB_SEARCH_TOOL_NAME;
</code></pre>
<p>Registered in config bootstrap (<code>packages/core/src/config/config.ts:3972-3973</code>):</p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">maybeRegister(WebSearchTool, () =>
  registry.registerTool(new WebSearchTool(this, this.messageBus)),
);
</code></pre>
<hr>
<h2>2. Execution pipeline (<code>WebSearchToolInvocation.execute</code>)</h2>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// 130_gemini-cli/packages/core/src/tools/web-search.ts:88-99
const response = await geminiClient.generateContent(
  { model: 'web-search' },
  [{ role: 'user', parts: [{ text: this.params.query }] }],
  signal,
  LlmRole.UTILITY_TOOL,
);
</code></pre>
<p>Post-processing (<code>:101-179</code>):</p>
<ol>
<li>Read <code>responseText</code> via <code>getResponseText(response)</code></li>
<li>Extract <code>groundingMetadata.groundingChunks</code> → source URIs/titles</li>
<li>Apply <code>groundingSupports</code> — insert <code>[n]</code> citation markers at UTF-8 byte positions (<code>:128-166</code>)</li>
<li>Append <code>Sources:\n[1] Title (uri)</code> footer (<code>:169-172</code>)</li>
<li>Return <code>{ llmContent, returnDisplay, sources }</code> (<code>:175-179</code>)</li>
</ol>
<p>Empty response path (<code>:111-116</code>) returns explicit "No information found" without throwing.</p>
<h3>Error handling</h3>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// web-search.ts:194-197
error: { message: errorMessage, type: ToolErrorType.WEB_SEARCH_FAILED }
</code></pre>
<p><code>ToolErrorType.WEB_SEARCH_FAILED = 'web_search_failed'</code> (<code>packages/core/src/tools/tool-error.ts:79</code>).</p>
<hr>
<h2>3. <code>web_fetch</code> companion tool</h2>
<p>Declared adjacent in <code>gemini-3.ts:412-427</code> — analyzes up to 20 URLs with a natural-language extraction prompt. Workflow documented in tool description: search with <code>google_web_search</code> → deep-read with <code>web_fetch</code> on returned URIs.</p>
<p><code>web_fetch.ts</code> reuses grounding metadata patterns (<code>:816-851</code>) for citation insertion on fetch results.</p>
<hr>
<h2>4. Policy engine integration</h2>
<p>Read-only policy auto-allows search (<code>packages/core/src/policy/policies/read-only.toml</code>):</p>
<pre><code class="language-toml">[[rule]]
toolName = "google_web_search"
decision = "allow"
</code></pre>
<p>Plan mode includes <code>google_web_search</code> in <code>auto_allow_tools</code> (<code>plan.toml</code>). Policy tests assert tool is not excluded (<code>policy-engine.test.ts:3075</code>, <code>:3166</code>).</p>
<hr>
<h2>5. Model config / API grounding hook</h2>
<p>Default model configs can attach native Google Search tool at API level:</p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">// packages/core/src/config/defaultModelConfigs.ts:213
tools: [{ googleSearch: {} }],
</code></pre>
<p>This is distinct from the declarative <code>google_web_search</code> <strong>agent tool</strong> — both paths relate to grounding but serve different layers (model config vs tool registry).</p>

<hr>
<h2>8. Server-side pipeline (Google API — not in CLI source)</h2>
<p>The CLI does not implement crawl/index/rank. Gemini API performs grounding when <code>model: 'web-search'</code> is invoked:</p>
<pre><code>Agent → google_web_search(query)
  → Gemini API (utility model)
  → [internal] Google Search + synthesis
  → groundingMetadata { groundingChunks, groundingSupports, webSearchQueries }
  → CLI formats citations + Sources footer
</code></pre>
<p>Pricing and quota are API-billing concerns (see Google AI docs); not encoded in <code>web-search.ts</code>.</p>
<hr>
<h2>Related corpus docs</h2>

<li>Harmonization: <code>000_overview/00_corpus_harmonization_status.md</code></li>
</ul>
<p>Pricing and quota are API-billing concerns (see Google AI docs); not encoded in <code>web-search.ts</code>.</p>
<hr>
<h2>9. Declarative tool metadata</h2>
<p><code>WebSearchTool</code> constructor registers with <code>Kind.Search</code> (<code>web-search.ts:220</code>) — groups the tool in scheduler/UI taxonomies alongside other search-class builtins.</p>
<p>Validation rejects empty queries before API call (<code>validateToolParamValues</code> <code>:233-239</code>):</p>
<pre><code class="language-typescript">if (!params.query || params.query.trim() === '') {
  return "The 'query' parameter cannot be empty.";
}
</code></pre>
<p><code>getSchema(modelId?)</code> delegates to <code>resolveToolDeclaration(WEB_SEARCH_DEFINITION, modelId)</code> (<code>:257-258</code>) so Gemini 2.x vs 3.x families can diverge declarations without duplicating execute logic.</p>
<p>Snapshot tests freeze declaration shape (<code>packages/core/src/tools/definitions/coreToolsModelSnapshots.test.ts:74</code>).</p>
<hr>
<h2>10. Citation insertion algorithm (client-side)</h2>
<p>Unlike Claude Code (server returns final blocks) or Codex (server streams <code>web_search_call</code>), Gemini CLI <strong>post-processes</strong> grounding on the client:</p>
<ol>
<li><strong>Chunk list</strong> — each <code>groundingChunks[i].web</code> yields <code>[i+1] Title (uri)</code> in Sources footer (<code>web-search.ts:121-126</code>)</li>
<li><strong>Inline markers</strong> — for each <code>groundingSupports</code> entry with <code>segment.endIndex</code> and <code>groundingChunkIndices</code>, build marker like <code>[1][2]</code> (<code>:131-138</code>)</li>
<li><strong>UTF-8 safe insertion</strong> — encode response to bytes, insert markers at descending indices to avoid offset drift (<code>:145-166</code>)</li>
<li><strong>Decode</strong> — <code>TextDecoder</code> restores final string with inline <code>[n]</code> markers before Sources block</li>
</ol>
<p>This means citation fidelity depends on API-provided byte indices matching response text encoding — the implementation explicitly uses <code>TextEncoder</code>/<code>TextDecoder</code> rather than JS string indices.</p>

<h2>12. Scheduler &#x26; agent loop context</h2>
<p><code>WebSearchToolInvocation</code> receives <code>AgentLoopContext</code> (<code>web-search.ts:74-75</code>) for <code>geminiClient</code> access. <code>LlmRole.UTILITY_TOOL</code> (<code>:98</code>) marks the sub-call as utility-tier in telemetry — distinct from main agent generation role.</p>
<p>Abort propagation: <code>isAbortError</code> → cancelled result without <code>WEB_SEARCH_FAILED</code> (<code>:181-185</code>).</p>

<hr>
<h2>14. <code>web_fetch</code> grounding reuse</h2>
<p><code>packages/core/src/tools/web-fetch.ts</code> duplicates grounding chunk/support handling for URL-batch fetch (<code>:816-851</code>). Shared pattern: extract <code>groundingMetadata</code>, map supports to citation markers, append source list. Web search and web fetch therefore share <strong>presentation logic</strong> for grounded answers even though fetch accepts URL prompts instead of search queries.</p>
<hr>
<h2>15. Registry resolution flow (end-to-end)</h2>
<pre><code>config.ts maybeRegister(WebSearchTool)
  → ToolRegistry.registerTool(new WebSearchTool(context, messageBus))
  → Agent issues function call google_web_search({ query })
  → WebSearchTool.createInvocation → WebSearchToolInvocation.execute
  → geminiClient.generateContent({ model: 'web-search' }, ...)
  → ToolResult.llmContent reinjected into main conversation
</code></pre>
<p>Model-family selection for the <strong>declaration</strong> seen by the main model:</p>
<pre><code>resolveToolDeclaration(WEB_SEARCH_DEFINITION, modelId)
  → coreTools.ts overrides per getToolSet(modelId)
  → gemini-3.ts or default-legacy.ts google_web_search block
</code></pre>
<p>The utility model id <code>'web-search'</code> in <code>execute()</code> is <strong>fixed</strong> and independent of the user's main chat model — similar in spirit to Claude Code's Haiku fast-path (<code>tengu_plum_vx3</code>) for search sub-calls.</p>

<h2>코퍼스 — 015_reverse-engineering/ (심화)</h2>
<h3><code>015_reverse-engineering/00_reverse_evidence_policy.md</code></h3>
<h1>Reverse Engineering Evidence Policy</h1>
<p>이 축은 설치 help parity 문서의 다음 단계다. 기존 <code>00</code>~<code>14</code> 축은 주로 help/config/local-doc 표면을 비교했고, 이 축은 설치된 바이너리와 번들에서 복원 가능한 구조를 따로 기록한다.</p>
<h2>Evidence Levels</h2>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Level</th>
<th>의미</th>
<th>사용할 수 있는 주장</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>installed-help</td>
<td><code>--help</code>, public command output, version output</td>
<td>명령/플래그/공개 subcommand가 존재한다</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>safe-local-doc</td>
<td>설치 패키지의 docs, changelog, examples, manifest</td>
<td>문서화된 schema/경로/기능 설명이 있다</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>bundle-key</td>
<td>minified bundle에 남은 module key, source path, route name, proto name</td>
<td>내부 모듈/라우터/프로토/컴포넌트가 존재한다</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>binary-string</td>
<td>native binary <code>strings</code>, <code>file</code>, <code>otool</code>, <code>codesign</code>, <code>nm</code></td>
<td>crate/package/protocol/tool/evaluator 이름이 embedded되어 있다</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>runtime-trace</td>
<td>synthetic project에서 실제 명령을 실행한 결과</td>
<td>동작 semantics, precedence, permission enforcement를 확인했다</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>private-artifact-name</td>
<td>비공개 상태 파일의 경로/개수만 관찰</td>
<td>artifact가 존재한다. 내용/schema 주장은 금지</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p><code>/Users/jun/Developer/codex/015_reverse-engineering/33_source_deobfuscation_inventory.md</code> further separates source-like recovery levels. In this corpus, Cursor reaches preserved module-key recovery, while Grok/Kiro/AGY mostly expose native source-path, handler, protobuf, and runtime-trace evidence. Do not call this "full source recovered" unless a real source map or readable source archive is present.</p>
<h2>Hard Boundary</h2>
<p>역분석의 목적은 제품 구조 복원이지 사용자 상태 추출이 아니다. 다음은 내용 읽기 금지다.</p>
<ul>
<li>auth/token/cookie/credential/login data</li>
<li>raw transcript, chat history, conversation DB/PB</li>
<li>logs and terminal captures</li>
<li>browser profile state, local storage, IndexedDB, session storage</li>
<li>memory/goal runtime stores</li>
<li>screenshots and browser recordings</li>
<li>private <code>mcp.json</code>, settings, config values unless explicitly redacted</li>
</ul>
<p>비공개 artifact는 “존재한다”까지만 쓴다. 필드/schema/content 주장은 public docs, source/bundle evidence, sanitized fixture, synthetic runtime trace가 있을 때만 쓴다.</p>

<h2>Reading Rule For Existing Docs</h2>
<p>When a <code>00</code>~<code>14</code> page says “없음” or “지원하지 않음”, interpret it as “installed help에서 노출되지 않음” unless this <code>15_reverse-engineering</code> axis confirms absence from bundle/binary evidence too.</p>
<p>When a page states runtime semantics from config/cache observation, this axis upgrades or downgrades the claim:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>bundle-key</code> or <code>binary-string</code> confirms a module exists.</li>
<li><code>runtime-trace</code> is still required for exact precedence, scheduling, isolation, merge, and permission behavior.</li>
</ul>

<h3><code>015_reverse-engineering/24_ki_agent_mcp_trace.md</code></h3>
<h1>Kiro Agent MCP Trace</h1>
<p>This pass used disposable temp <code>HOME</code> and workspace directories. It did not run model prompts, start real MCP servers, authenticate, or read private Kiro sessions.</p>
<h2>Public Help Surface</h2>
<p>Commands inspected:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>/Users/jun/.local/bin/kiro-cli-chat agent create --help</code></li>
<li><code>/Users/jun/.local/bin/kiro-cli-chat agent list --help</code></li>
<li><code>/Users/jun/.local/bin/kiro-cli-chat mcp add --help</code></li>
<li><code>/Users/jun/.local/bin/kiro-cli-chat mcp list --help</code></li>
</ul>
<p>Relevant help semantics:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>agent create [NAME] --directory &#x3C;DIRECTORY></code> creates an agent config in the chosen directory, but opens an editor by default.</li>
<li><code>agent list</code> says local agents are discovered only when invoked in a directory that contains them.</li>
<li><code>mcp add --agent &#x3C;AGENT></code> writes the server to the named agent.</li>
<li><code>mcp add --scope &#x3C;SCOPE></code> is only meaningful when no agent name is supplied.</li>
</ul>
<h2>Editor Behavior</h2>
<p><code>agent create trace --directory &#x3C;tmp>/ws/.kiro/agents</code> created <code>&#x3C;tmp>/ws/.kiro/agents/trace.json</code> and opened it in <code>vi</code>. The generated template shape was:</p>
<pre><code class="language-json">{
  "name": "trace",
  "description": "",
  "prompt": null,
  "mcpServers": {},
  "tools": ["*"],
  "toolAliases": {},
  "allowedTools": [],
  "resources": [],
  "hooks": {},
  "toolsSettings": {},
  "includeMcpJson": true,
  "model": null
}
</code></pre>
<p>The editor process was terminated after capturing the template. Follow-up traces used a directly written synthetic JSON file with the same shape to avoid interactive editor state.</p>
<h2>Workspace Agent Discovery</h2>

<h2>Documentation Consequences</h2>
<ul>
<li>Kiro has a public no-model path for validating custom workspace agents and binding MCP servers to a specific agent.</li>
<li><code>--agent &#x3C;name></code> overrides <code>--scope</code>; agent-specific MCP config is stored inside the agent JSON rather than the workspace <code>.kiro/settings/mcp.json</code> path observed for non-agent workspace MCP.</li>
<li><code>includeMcpJson: true</code> is present in the generated agent template, but this trace does not prove its runtime inclusion semantics.</li>

</code></pre>

<h2>Remaining Gaps</h2>

<h3><code>015_reverse-engineering/32_agy_agentapi_route_trace.md</code></h3>
<h1>AGY AgentAPI Route Trace</h1>
<p>This pass inspected the installed AGY binary and public wrapper only. It did not authenticate, read private AGY logs, read private conversations, or send Agent API messages.</p>
<h2>Wrapper Identity</h2>
<p>Only one installed Agent API wrapper was found under the Antigravity CLI home:</p>
<pre><code class="language-text">/Users/jun/.gemini/antigravity-cli/bin/agentapi
</code></pre>
<p><code>file</code> classified it as:</p>
<pre><code class="language-text">/Users/jun/.gemini/antigravity-cli/bin/agentapi: POSIX shell script text executable, ASCII text
/Users/jun/.local/bin/agy:                           Mach-O 64-bit executable arm64
/Users/jun/.gemini/antigravity-cli/bin/webm_encoder: Mach-O 64-bit executable arm64
</code></pre>
<p>The wrapper contents are:</p>
<pre><code class="language-sh">#!/bin/sh
exec "/Users/jun/.local/bin/agy" agentapi "$@"
</code></pre>
<p>This proves that AGY installs an <code>agentapi</code> executable shim, but not that the public top-level router currently accepts <code>agentapi</code>.</p>
<h2>Public Router Behavior</h2>
<p>Direct public route:</p>
<pre><code class="language-text">/Users/jun/.local/bin/agy agentapi --help
</code></pre>
<p>returned exit <code>0</code>, but printed only top-level AGY help. The available subcommands listed were:</p>
<pre><code class="language-text">changelog
help
install
plugin
plugins
update
</code></pre>
<p>No <code>agentapi</code> subcommand help, handler list, or Agent API command schema was exposed.</p>
<p>Explicit help lookup:</p>
<pre><code class="language-text">/Users/jun/.local/bin/agy help agentapi
</code></pre>
<p>returned exit <code>1</code> with:</p>
<pre><code class="language-text">Error: unknown subcommand: agentapi
</code></pre>
<p>The wrapper path behaves the same because it execs <code>/Users/jun/.local/bin/agy agentapi "$@"</code>. Therefore the current installed public CLI surface has a wrapper/script for <code>agentapi</code>, but the direct public subcommand route is not active in normal no-context invocation.</p>
<h2>Binary String Evidence</h2>
<p>The AGY Mach-O binary still contains first-class Agent API implementation strings and prompt templates. Relevant hits include:</p>
<pre><code class="language-text">usage: agentapi %s %s
failed to write agentapi script
failed to format agentapi script
exec "%s" agentapi "$@"
agentapi new-conversation "Help me fix this bug"
agentapi get-conversation-metadata "some-conversation-id"
agentapi new-conversation --model=%s "Run a complex refactor"
agentapi send-message "&#x3C;other-conversation-id>" "Task completed successfully"
agentapi send-message "&#x3C;your-conversation-id>" "Reminder: check build status"
You have access to the Agent API CLI tool: 'agentapi', which contains subcommands for interacting with Agent API.
subprocess.run(["agentapi", subcommand, arg1, arg2])
- **events/** (Generated): For every agentapi call, a timestamped .json file is created in the events/ subdirectory.
- Background sidecars can use the agentapi CLI tool to programmatically interact with the system.
google3/third_party/jetski/cortex/agentapi/agentapi.RegisterHandler
google3/third_party/jetski/cortex/agentapi/agentapi.(*sendMessageHandler).Execute
google3/third_party/jetski/cortex/agentapi/agentapi.(*newConversationHandler).Execute
google3/third_party/jetski/cortex/agentapi/agentapi.(*getConversationMetadataHandler).Execute
google3/third_party/jetski/cortex/agentapi/agentapi.(*sendMessageHandler).Metadata
google3/third_party/jetski/cortex/agentapi/agentapi.(*newConversationHandler).Metadata
google3/third_party/jetski/cortex/agentapi/agentapi.(*getConversationMetadataHandler).Metadata
google3/third_party/jetski/cortex/agentapi/agentapi.GetHandlerNames
google3/third_party/jetski/cortex/agentapi/agentapi.GetHandler
</code></pre>
<p>This changes the conclusion from "agentapi unknown" to "Agent API implementation exists in the binary, but the installed public wrapper does not expose it as a normal subcommand without the right runtime context."</p>
<h2>MCP / Browser Linkage</h2>
<p>The same binary contains browser/MCP bridge strings adjacent to Agent API sidecar strings:</p>
<pre><code class="language-text">McpBrowserRecordingStopHook: Failed to send agentapi message (output: %s)
google3/third_party/jetski/cortex/executors/posttoolhooks/posttoolhooks.NewMcpBrowserRecordingStopHook
/exa.extension_server_pb.ExtensionServerService/GetChromeDevtoolsMcpUrl
GetChromeDevtoolsMcpUrlRequest
GetChromeDevtoolsMcpUrlResponse
GetChromeDevtoolsMcpUrl
RefreshMcpServers
ToggleMcpServer
GetMcpServerStates
CompleteMcpOAuth
</code></pre>
<p>This is binary-level evidence that Agent API, browser recording hooks, Chrome DevTools MCP URL plumbing, and MCP server state/OAuth controls are connected inside AGY's runtime. It is not a proof that a no-auth standalone shell can call those paths.</p>
<h2>Interpretation</h2>
<p>AGY has two separable surfaces:</p>
<table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Surface</th>
<th>Status</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Installed wrapper</td>
<td>confirmed at <code>/Users/jun/.gemini/antigravity-cli/bin/agentapi</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Direct public CLI route</td>
<td>not exposed in normal no-context invocation; <code>help agentapi</code> says unknown</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Binary Agent API implementation</td>
<td>confirmed by handler, command, prompt-template, sidecar, and generated-events strings</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Known subcommand names from strings</td>
<td><code>send-message</code>, <code>new-conversation</code>, <code>get-conversation-metadata</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Working command invocation</td>
<td>not confirmed without authenticated/runtime context</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<p>The most likely model is that AGY writes or enables the <code>agentapi</code> shim for background sidecars or agent runtime contexts, while normal top-level <code>agy agentapi</code> is not a documented public command in the current installed build.</p>
<h2>Named Subcommand Help Probe</h2>
<p>A disposable HOME probe through the installed wrapper confirmed that known binary subcommand names still do not expose public help:</p>
<pre><code class="language-text">HOME=/tmp/... /Users/jun/.gemini/antigravity-cli/bin/agentapi send-message --help
HOME=/tmp/... /Users/jun/.gemini/antigravity-cli/bin/agentapi new-conversation --help
HOME=/tmp/... /Users/jun/.gemini/antigravity-cli/bin/agentapi get-conversation-metadata --help
</code></pre>
<p>All three exited <code>0</code> but printed only top-level AGY help with the public subcommand list <code>changelog</code>, <code>help</code>, <code>install</code>, <code>plugin</code>, <code>plugins</code>, and <code>update</code>. This tightens the boundary: <code>send-message</code>, <code>new-conversation</code>, and <code>get-conversation-metadata</code> are binary handler names, not no-context public CLI routes in this install.</p>
<h2>Sidecar Contract Strings</h2>
<p>The binary also exposes a sidecar configuration/runtime vocabulary adjacent to Agent API examples:</p>
<ul>
<li>sidecar root examples: <code>sidecars/</code>, <code>sidecar_data/</code>, one folder per sidecar ID, required <code>sidecar.json</code></li>
<li>config fields: <code>command</code>, <code>builtin</code>, <code>restart_policy</code>, <code>args</code>, <code>description</code>, <code>has_web_ui</code>, <code>env</code>, <code>display_name</code>, <code>disabled</code>, <code>ui_config</code></li>
<li>runtime directories: <code>data/</code>, <code>logs/</code>, <code>events/</code></li>
<li>runtime environment: <code>ANTIGRAVITY_EXECUTABLE_DATA_DIR</code>, <code>ANTIGRAVITY_SIDECAR_WEB_PORT</code></li>
<li>builtin scheduler shape: <code>schedule</code> with args like <code>["&#x3C;cron_schedule>", "&#x3C;command>", "&#x3C;arg1>", ...]</code></li>
<li>schedule syntax examples: five-field cron, <code>@hourly</code>, <code>@daily</code>, <code>@every 1h</code>, <code>@every 30m</code></li>
<li>schema names: <code>SidecarUserConfig</code>, <code>SidecarStatusInfo</code>, <code>SidecarUIConfig</code>, <code>SidecarUIView</code>, <code>SidecarUIEntrypoint</code></li>
</ul>
<p>This supports the interpretation that Agent API is intended for sidecar/runtime contexts. It still does not expose the activation environment or output schema for safe no-context calls.</p>
<h2>Remaining Gaps</h2>
<ul>
<li>Whether <code>agentapi</code> becomes active only with specific environment variables, app-data directory state, sidecar context, or authenticated project runtime.</li>
<li>Exact arguments and JSON output schema for <code>send-message</code>, <code>new-conversation</code>, and <code>get-conversation-metadata</code>.</li>
<li>Whether <code>events/*.json</code> are written under a temp runtime directory, an app-data directory, or a conversation-specific directory.</li>
<li>Whether background scheduled tasks can safely invoke <code>agentapi</code> from <code>PATH</code> without going through <code>agy agentapi</code>.</li>
<li>Whether <code>McpBrowserRecordingStopHook</code> sends messages via Agent API only after a live browser/MCP recording session.</li>
<li>Whether Agent API is stable user-facing contract or internal sidecar contract.</li>
</ul>

<h2>000/00_grand_synthesis.md (발췌)</h2>
<h1>GRAND SYNTHESIS — 5개 코딩 에이전트 × 13개 차원 최종 종합 분석</h1>
<p>이 문서는 Codex, Aider, Gemini CLI, OpenCode, Claude Code를 13개 아키텍처 차원에서 동시에 비교한 캡스톤 문서다.
개별 비교 문서의 결론을 단순 재배열하지 않고, 서로 다른 설계 철학이 어떤 제품 전략으로 수렴하는지까지 읽어내는 것을 목표로 한다.</p>
<pre><code class="language-mermaid">graph TD
    A[5개 에이전트 개요] --> B[13개 차원 비교]
    B --> C[공통 패턴 추출]
    B --> D[핵심 차별점 추출]
    C --> E[기술 선택 시사점]
    D --> E
    E --> F[미래 전망과 설계 교훈]
</code></pre>
<h2>1. 개요</h2>
<h3>이 문서의 목적</h3>
<p>이 문서의 목적은 5개 에이전트를 한 번에 조망할 수 있는 상위 레퍼런스를 만드는 것이다.
개별 문서는 특정 축의 우열을 설명하지만, 실제 제품 선택은 언제나 여러 축의 동시 판단을 요구한다.
따라서 여기서는 TUI, prompt, tool, skill, subagent, app-server, sandbox, config, MCP, memory, plugin, guardian, 그리고 잔여 교차 관심사를 하나의 프레임으로 다시 묶는다.</p>
<ul>
<li>근거: [[00_co_overview]], [[00_ai_overview]], [[00_ge_overview]], [[00_oc_overview]], [[00_cc_overview]]</li>
</ul>
<h3>분석 범위</h3>
<p>범위는 5개 에이전트와 13개 차원이다.
에이전트는 Codex, Aider, Gemini CLI, OpenCode, Claude Code다.
차원은 TUI, Prompt/Context, Tool Runtime, Skill, Subagents, App-Server Surface, Sandbox, Config, MCP, Memory, Plugin, Guardian, 잔여 교차 관심사(Git/VCS, 모델 라우팅, 에러 처리, 텔레메트리, IDE 통합, 패키징, 테스트, 인증, 멀티모달, 이벤트 시스템, 피처 플래그, 국제화)다.
App-Server 축은 비교 문서 자체가 Codex·Gemini CLI·OpenCode 중심으로 작성되어 있으므로 Aider와 Claude Code는 “의도적 부재”까지 함께 해석한다.</p>
<ul>
<li>근거: [[001_tui-design/00_tui]], [[002_prompt-context/00_prompt]], [[003_tool-runtime/00_tool]], [[004_skill-system/00_skill]], [[005_subagents-collab/00_subagent]], [[006_app-server-client-surfaces/00_surface]], [[007_sandbox-exec-policy/00_sandbox]], [[008_config-system/00_config]], [[009_mcp-orchestration/00_mcp]], [[010_memory-pipeline/00_memory]], [[011_plugin-system/00_plugin]], [[012_guardian-approval/00_guardian]], [[013_etc/00_etc]]</li>
</ul>
<h3>분석 방법론</h3>
<p>첫째, 각 에이전트 개요 문서에서 기술 스택, 패키지 구조, 핵심 철학을 추출했다.
둘째, 13개 비교 문서에서 축별 우위와 결손, 스카우팅 점수, 디자인 패턴을 수집했다.
셋째, 같은 에이전트가 여러 축에서 반복적으로 보이는 패턴을 묶어 장기 전략으로 재해석했다.
넷째, 단일 승자를 찾기보다 “어떤 상황에서 어떤 설계가 더 설득력 있는가”를 기준으로 실무 추천안을 도출했다.</p>
<ul>
<li>근거: [[00_co_overview]], [[00_ai_overview]], [[00_ge_overview]], [[00_oc_overview]], [[00_cc_overview]], [[001_tui-design/00_tui]], [[012_guardian-approval/00_guardian]]</li>
</ul>
<h3>이 문서를 읽는 방법</h3>
<p>제품 선택이 목적이면 3장, 7장, 8장을 먼저 보는 것이 좋다.
포크나 재구현이 목적이면 2장, 5장, 6장, 9장을 먼저 보는 것이 좋다.
보안 검토가 목적이면 3장, 4장, 8장, 9장을 함께 읽는 편이 낫다.
마지막 부록은 문서 인덱스 역할을 하므로 세부 원문으로 돌아갈 때 사용하면 된다.</p>
<ul>
<li>근거: [[007_sandbox-exec-policy/00_sandbox]], [[009_mcp-orchestration/00_mcp]], [[011_plugin-system/00_plugin]], [[012_guardian-approval/00_guardian]]</li>
</ul>

<h2>2. 에이전트 프로필 요약</h2>

<tr>
<td>Codex</td>
<td>Rust + TypeScript + React/Ink + app-server protocol</td>
<td>엔진을 층으로 분리하고, prompt·tool·skill·subagent·MCP를 제어면(control plane)으로 다룬다.</td>
<td>가장 분해 가능한 core engine, 가장 강한 terminal-native orchestration, 가장 균형 잡힌 sandbox/MCP 결합.</td>
<td>보안, 오케스트레이션, 포크 가능한 core engine이 중요한 팀</td>
<td>[[00_co_overview]], [[001_tui-design/00_tui]], [[002_prompt-context/00_prompt]]</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Aider</td>
<td>Python + prompt_toolkit + rich + tree-sitter + Git</td>
<td>도구 플랫폼보다 코드 편집 루프에 집중한다. 모델을 좋은 editor로 만드는 쪽에 최적화한다.</td>
<td>RepoMap, edit 전략 다양성, git auto-commit, 최소 마찰 CLI 경험.</td>
<td>개인 개발자, 빠른 코드 편집, 낮은 학습 비용이 중요한 사용 사례</td>
<td>[[00_ai_overview]], [[001_tui-design/00_tui]], [[002_prompt-context/00_prompt]]</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Gemini CLI</td>
<td>TypeScript + React/Ink + Zod + A2A server + multi-package monorepo</td>
<td>schema-first와 policy-first를 결합해 CLI를 확장 운영체계처럼 다룬다.</td>
<td>PromptProvider/Scheduler/PolicyEngine/ModelRouter/ExtensionManager가 분리된 가장 운영형 TypeScript engine.</td>
<td>엔터프라이즈 CLI, 확장 운영, 정책 감사, TypeScript 기반 재구현</td>
<td>[[00_ge_overview]], [[001_tui-design/00_tui]], [[004_skill-system/00_skill]]</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>OpenCode</td>
<td>TypeScript + Bun + Effect-TS + Hono + SolidJS + Tauri</td>
<td>agent runtime을 웹/데스크톱/SDK가 공유하는 product platform으로 본다.</td>
<td>Effect-TS service layer, 21+ provider, plugin SDK, session replay, multi-surface delivery.</td>
<td>빠른 제품화, GUI/desktop 포함, TS로 직접 확장하고 싶은 팀</td>
<td>[[00_oc_overview]], [[001_tui-design/00_tui]], [[003_tool-runtime/00_tool]]</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Claude Code</td>
<td>TypeScript/JavaScript bundle + React/Ink + custom renderer + Anthropic runtime</td>
<td>제품 사용성을 최우선으로 하면서 hook, security chain, memory, MCP를 깊게 묶는다.</td>
<td>가장 풍부한 productized tool surface, deepest shell security, strongest file-based memory UX.</td>
<td>상용 CLI UX, 강한 shell security, memory-heavy workflows, enterprise policy integration</td>
<td>[[00_cc_overview]], [[001_tui-design/00_tui]], [[005_subagents-collab/00_subagent]]</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h3>Codex</h3>
<ul>
<li>정체성: 엔진을 층으로 분리하고, prompt·tool·skill·subagent·MCP를 제어면(control plane)으로 다룬다.</li>
<li>기술 스택: Rust + TypeScript + React/Ink + app-server protocol</li>
<li>핵심 차별점: 가장 분해 가능한 core engine, 가장 강한 terminal-native orchestration, 가장 균형 잡힌 sandbox/MCP 결합.</li>
<li>실무에서 강한 상황: 보안, 오케스트레이션, 포크 가능한 core engine이 중요한 팀</li>
<li>재구현 관점 한 줄 평: requirements 제약 채널과 prompt fragment provenance를 분리한 구조.</li>
<li>근거: [[00_co_overview]], [[001_tui-design/00_tui]], [[002_prompt-context/00_prompt]], [[003_tool-runtime/00_tool]], [[005_subagents-collab/00_subagent]], [[007_sandbox-exec-policy/00_sandbox]], [[009_mcp-orchestration/00_mcp]]</li>
</ul>
<h3>Aider</h3>
<ul>
<li>정체성: 도구 플랫폼보다 코드 편집 루프에 집중한다. 모델을 좋은 editor로 만드는 쪽에 최적화한다.</li>
<li>기술 스택: Python + prompt_toolkit + rich + tree-sitter + Git</li>
<li>핵심 차별점: RepoMap, edit 전략 다양성, git auto-com</li>
</ul>
